Berserk

Its a dark anime and one of my favorite.of my friend suggest me after.It has violation, complecated story as well as enriched story,adult scenes and etc.But author had died before finish it and its matter of sorrow that masterpice was unfinished.The mc was a normal guy with having some kind of phobia.When he was kid he had to do mercencery job and bear other baggage to maintain his livelhood. Many thing happend durring his journey.I dont wanna spoil the fun you should watch it. Some perks and cons are given below.

  1. Good character development
  2. Unique good story
  3. Anime adaptin isn't quite good but manga is best
  4. Only problem is its unfinished


Watch now on gogoanime


Tokyo Ghoul

Tokyo ghoul is quite twisted anime.Its a story about a simple boy who one's date a ghoul(worst luck and pathetic).That day change his life entirely.He became a rare one eyed ghoul with special ability.Here starts his struggle to become one with his new strength.Here some topic I like most:

  1. Character development(simple to good hearted matured person).
  2. Twisted story
